Kubernetes API Server Audit Logging Implementation\\n\\nThe Kubernetes API server implements a comprehensive audit logging system across multiple Go packages in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository. Here is a complete breakdown of the implementation:\\n\\n## 1. Audit Event Creation from Requests\\n\\nThe audit event creation process starts with HTTP request filters that initialize and capture audit information:\\n\\n**Request Initialization & ID Generation:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/audit_init.go:WithAuditInit` - Initializes audit context with a unique audit ID for each request. If the client doesn't provide an Audit-ID header, a new UUID is generated. The audit ID is echoed back in the response header.\\n\\n**Main Audit Filter:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/audit.go:WithAudit` - The primary audit filter decorator that wraps HTTP handlers. It calls `evaluatePolicyAndCreateAuditEvent` to initialize the audit context with the appropriate policy configuration.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/audit.go:evaluatePolicyAndCreateAuditEvent` - Evaluates the audit policy against request attributes and initializes the AuditContext with the policy configuration and sink.\\n\\n**Failed Authentication Audit:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/authn_audit.go:WithFailedAuthenticationAudit` - Specialized filter for auditing failed authentication attempts.\\n\\n**Audit Context Management:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/context.go:AuditContext` - Manages the audit event object for a request, including user info, resource references, and request/response metadata.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/context.go:ProcessEventStage` - Processes audit events at different request stages (RequestReceived, ResponseStarted, ResponseComplete, Panic).\\n\\n**Request/Response Logging:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/request.go:LogRequestMetadata` - Captures request metadata (URI, verb, user, source IPs, resource references).\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/request.go:LogRequestObject` - Captures the request body object at the appropriate audit level.\\n- Related functions in request.go for logging impersonated users, request patches, and response objects.\\n\\n## 2. Audit Policy Evaluation\\n\\nThe audit policy system determines which requests should be audited and at what level:\\n\\n**Policy Evaluation:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/evaluator.go:PolicyRuleEvaluator` - Interface that evaluates audit policy rules against request attributes.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/checker.go:NewPolicyRuleEvaluator` - Creates a policy rule evaluator from an audit policy.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/checker.go:EvaluatePolicyRule` - Evaluates each policy rule by checking users, groups, verbs, namespaces, resources, and non-resource URLs. Returns the audit level (None, Metadata, Request, RequestResponse) and stages to omit.\\n\\n**Policy File Handling:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/reader.go:LoadPolicyFromFile` - Reads and parses the audit policy YAML file.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/util.go` - Utility functions for policy matching including pattern matching for URLs and resource wildcards.\\n\\n## 3. Audit Backend Dispatch\\n\\nThe audit backend system dispatches events to multiple destinations (log files and webhooks):\\n\\n**Core Backend Interfaces:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/types.go:Backend` - Interface that extends Sink with Run() and Shutdown() methods. Every backend must implement ProcessEvents, Run, Shutdown, and String().\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/types.go:Sink` - Interface with ProcessEvents(events) method for handling audit events.\\n\\n**Union Backend (Multi-Backend Dispatch):**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/union.go:Union` - Creates a composite backend that sends events to multiple backends sequentially. Allows combining log file and webhook backends.\\n\\n**Log File Backend:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/log/backend.go:NewBackend` - Creates a log file backend that writes audit events to a file.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/log/backend.go:ProcessEvents` - Encodes and writes events in either legacy (1-line text) or JSON format.\\n\\n**Webhook Backend:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/webhook/webhook.go:NewBackend` - Creates a webhook backend configured from a file.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/webhook/webhook.go:NewDynamicBackend` - Creates a webhook backend from a REST client for dynamic webhook configuration.\\n- The webhook backend sends audit events via HTTP POST requests to external audit services with exponential backoff retry logic.\\n\\n**Buffered Backend (Event Batching):**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/buffered/buffered.go:NewBackend` - Wraps a delegate backend with buffering and batching capabilities.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/buffered/buffered.go:ProcessEvents` - Collects events into batches and sends them to the delegate backend asynchronously or synchronously based on configuration. Supports batching modes (batch, blocking, blocking-strict) with throttling.\\n\\n## 4. Audit Truncation for Large Events\\n\\nThe truncation system prevents oversized events from being lost:\\n\\n**Truncation Backend:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/truncate/truncate.go:NewBackend` - Creates a truncating backend that wraps a delegate backend.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/truncate/truncate.go:ProcessEvents` - Checks event size and batch size against configured limits. Implementation\\n\\nThe Kubernetes API server implements a comprehensive audit logging system across multiple Go packages in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository. Here is a complete breakdown of the implementation:\\n\\n## 1. Audit Event Creation from Requests\\n\\nThe audit event creation process starts with HTTP request filters that initialize and capture audit information:\\n\\n**Request Initialization & ID Generation:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/audit_init.go:WithAuditInit` - Initializes audit context with a unique audit ID for each request. If the client doesn't provide an Audit-ID header, a new UUID is generated. The audit ID is echoed back in the response header.\\n\\n**Main Audit Filter:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/audit.go:WithAudit` - The primary audit filter decorator that wraps HTTP handlers. It calls `evaluatePolicyAndCreateAuditEvent` to initialize the audit context with the appropriate policy configuration.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/audit.go:evaluatePolicyAndCreateAuditEvent` - Evaluates the audit policy against request attributes and initializes the AuditContext with the policy configuration and sink.\\n\\n**Failed Authentication Audit:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/authn_audit.go:WithFailedAuthenticationAudit` - Specialized filter for auditing failed authentication attempts.\\n\\n**Audit Context Management:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/context.go:AuditContext` - Manages the audit event object for a request, including user info, resource references, and request/response metadata.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/context.go:ProcessEventStage` - Processes audit events at different request stages (RequestReceived, ResponseStarted, ResponseComplete, Panic).\\n\\n**Request/Response Logging:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/request.go:LogRequestMetadata` - Captures request metadata (URI, verb, user, source IPs, resource references).\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/request.go:LogRequestObject` - Captures the request body object at the appropriate audit level.\\n- Related functions in request.go for logging impersonated users, request patches, and response objects.\\n\\n## 2. Audit Policy Evaluation\\n\\nThe audit policy system determines which requests should be audited and at what level:\\n\\n**Policy Evaluation:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/evaluator.go:PolicyRuleEvaluator` - Interface that evaluates audit policy rules against request attributes.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/checker.go:NewPolicyRuleEvaluator` - Creates a policy rule evaluator from an audit policy.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/checker.go:EvaluatePolicyRule` - Evaluates each policy rule by checking users, groups, verbs, namespaces, resources, and non-resource URLs. Returns the audit level (None, Metadata, Request, RequestResponse) and stages to omit.\\n\\n**Policy File Handling:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/reader.go:LoadPolicyFromFile` - Reads and parses the audit policy YAML file.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/util.go` - Utility functions for policy matching including pattern matching for URLs and resource wildcards.\\n\\n## 3. Audit Backend Dispatch\\n\\nThe audit backend system dispatches events to multiple destinations (log files and webhooks):\\n\\n**Core Backend Interfaces:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/types.go:Backend` - Interface that extends Sink with Run() and Shutdown() methods. Every backend must implement ProcessEvents, Run, Shutdown, and String().\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/types.go:Sink` - Interface with ProcessEvents(events) method for handling audit events.\\n\\n**Union Backend (Multi-Backend Dispatch):**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/union.go:Union` - Creates a composite backend that sends events to multiple backends sequentially. Allows combining log file and webhook backends.\\n\\n**Log File Backend:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/log/backend.go:NewBackend` - Creates a log file backend that writes audit events to a file.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/log/backend.go:ProcessEvents` - Encodes and writes events in either legacy (1-line text) or JSON format.\\n\\n**Webhook Backend:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/webhook/webhook.go:NewBackend` - Creates a webhook backend configured from a file.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/webhook/webhook.go:NewDynamicBackend` - Creates a webhook backend from a REST client for dynamic webhook configuration.\\n- The webhook backend sends audit events via HTTP POST requests to external audit services with exponential backoff retry logic.\\n\\n**Buffered Backend (Event Batching):**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/buffered/buffered.go:NewBackend` - Wraps a delegate backend with buffering and batching capabilities.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/buffered/buffered.go:ProcessEvents` - Collects events into batches and sends them to the delegate backend asynchronously or synchronously based on configuration. Supports batching modes (batch, blocking, blocking-strict) with throttling.\\n\\n## 4.
